 28th of February is a day to celebrate the important achievements of Indian science world
 ji haa aaj rashtriya vigyaan diwas he
 The 'raman Effect' was discovered on this day
 isiilie aaj is diwas ko manaaya jaataa he
 The Raman effect was discovered by the great physicist Sir Chandrasekhar Venkata Raman (CV Raman)
 is mahatvapurn khoj ke liye sivi raman ko 1930 main bhautikee ke nobel puraskaar se sammanit kiya gaya tha
 National Science Day has been celebrated in honor of this discovery since 1986
 sar sivi raman kaa janm british bharat main tatkaaleen madras presidency (tamilnadu) main saat november 1888 ko hua tha
 He made an incredible contribution in the field of light scattering
 iske tahat jab prakaash kisi paardarshee material se gujarata he to us dauraan prakaash kii tarangadairdhya main badlaav dikhataa he
 This is called the Raman effect
 is mahatvapurn khoj ke liye 1954 main bharat ne unako sarvocch sammaan bharat ratna se nawaja
 The comments 1917 main sarkari naukari se istipha dene ke baad vah kalakatta uniwarsity main professor ho gaye
 During that time he continued his research work at the Indian Association for the Cultivation of Science (IACS) in Calcutta
 yaheen par 28 farvari, 1928 ko unhone kees krishnan samet anya vaigyanikon ke saath milakar raman prabhaav kii khoj kii
 CV Raman was the uncle of the famous scientist Subramanian Chandrasekhar
 'chandrashekhar limit' kii khoj ke liye subramanyan ko 1983 main nobel puraskaar diya gaya
 CV Raman died in 1970 at the age of 82

 is film main jon abraham (john Abraham) disipi sanjeev kumaar kii bhoomika nibhaa rahe hai jinpar farji encounter kaa aarope laga tha
 There was an investigation on the Batla House encounter and still the court's decision on the issue is awaited

 Through this film, viewers will be able to watch the story of this Batla House encounter
 is film main sabase khaas baat yah he ki 'bottla house (batla House)' kii story ko achche se research karke iskaa screenple taiyaar kiya gaya he
 Everyone's perspective in the film is well shown, including the views of human rights, police, ngos, media and general public
 iske alaava 'bottla house (batla House)' har sawaal kaa jawaab bhi bakhubi de rahi he, jaise 'ek ladke ke sir par goli kaise lagi? or itani suraksha ke hote hue do log bhaage kaise?' haalanki, film kii puri kahani ek police vaale ke najariye se hi aage badhati he

 movie main jon abraham (john Abraham) ne disipi sanjeev kumaar kii bhoomika behtareen tareeke se nibhaai he

 acting se itar film kii cinemetography bhi behtareen he or isaki editing bhi bahut achche se kii gai he

 khaas taur se pehle half main kuch drishy kam yaa chote karke 5 se 7 minute kam kiye ja sakate the
 Even after the interval, the film drags at some places

 tamaam film magagenes or akhabaaron ne is afaire ke bare main likhaa

 sanjay us samay richa sharma se shaadishuda the

 hina or rocky goa ke liye ravaanaa hone ke liye mumbai airport par najar aae
 Hina Khan appeared in a sporty casual look at the airport
 hina mini skirt main kute dikhin or rocky bhi looj pants main confort luk main dikhe
 The body of Sarabjit Singh, an Indian prisoner who died in the hospital, has reached his native village Bhikhiwind
 yahaan se postmortem ke liye pattee le jaaya gaya
 After the post mortem, the body is said to be brought back to the village late at night
 aaj yahaan par puure rajkeey sammaan ke saath antim sanskaar kiya jayega
 Many big leaders will be present at the funeral
 isse pehle air india ke vishesh vimaan se sarbajit ke shav ko amritsar ke hawaii adde par laayaa gaya
 At first it was expected that due to the darkness, the body would be taken to the village by helicopter but later another helicopter was flown along which arranged the lights and made it easier to fly
 bhikhivind se 15-16 kilometre kii duuri par pattee he jahaan par shav kaa postmortem kiya gaya
 Two Union Ministers Manish Tiwari and Parneet Kaur along with some Ministers and officials of the State Government are also present at Amritsar Airport
 punjab sarkaar ne teen din ke rajkeey shok kii ghoshnaa kii he
 The Punjab government, with the help of one crore rupees, has promised to give government jobs to both the daughters of Sarabjit
 iske alaava punjab sarkaar ne sarbajit ko shahid kaa darja bhi diya he
 a financial aid of Rs 25 lakh has been announced by the central government
 vahiin, guuruuvaar kii shaam pakistan se khabar thi ki custom vibhaag ne kuch kagajaton ke abhaav main airport par hi sarbajit ke shav ko roak liya tha
 He said that NOC has not been given yet from the Ministry of External Affairs
 baad main kagaji kaarywahi puri ho hone ke baad vimaan sarbajit kaa shav lekar uda or amritsar ke hawaii adde par kareeb 7
 Arrived at 30 o'clock
 shuukravaar ko rajkeey sammaan ke saath sarbajit kaa antim sanskaar kareeb do baje kiya jayega
 It is also being said that Prime Minister Manmohan Singh is also expected to attend the funeral
 inke alaava congress party ke upaadhyaksh rahul gandhi bhi sarbajit ke antim sanskaar main shaamil honge
 It is noteworthy that while struggling between life and death for a week, Sarabjit breathed his last at 12:45 pm on Wednesday
 sarbajit kaa lahore ke jinna aspataal main dil kaa daura padane se nidhan ho gaya
 He died after being in a deep coma for the last six days after a brutal assault by inmates in a tight-security prison
 pakistan sarkaar ne sarbajit ke postmortem ke liye doctoron kaa ek panel gathit kiya tha
 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh lamented the death of Sarabjit Singh and said that the culprits responsible for the barbaric and murderous attack on Sarabjit should be brought to justice
 videsh mantralay ne ek press relies jari kar kaha ki sarbajit ke saath jo kuch bhi hua, usase bharat sarkaar behad aahat he
 India considers the attack on Sarabjit a murderous attack on an Indian citizen and wants the Pakistan government to conduct an impartial inquiry and take strict action against the culprits
 saath hi videsh mantralay ne pakistan kii jelon main band bhartiya kaidiyon kii suraksha ko lekar vahaan kii sarkaar se kadam uthaane kii maang bhi kii he
 Congress Vice President Rahul Gandhi met Sarabjit's family
 sutron ne bataaya ki gandhi ne sarbajit ke parivaar ke saath kareeb 40 minute bitaye or unhen santvanaa di
 Union Home Minister Sushil Kumar Shinde also met Sarabjit's family
 sarbajit kii bahan dalbir cor or parivaar ke duusare sadasyon se mulaakaat karne ke baad scindia ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha ki shav mil jane ke baad parivaar kii bhaawanaaon ke anusaar antim sanskaar kiya jayega
 Shinde said that India kept talking to Pakistan till the last time to ensure better treatment for 49-year-old Sarabjit, but could not succeed
 unhone kaha ki maine puure desh kii ore se sarbajit ke bahan ke prati samvednaa prakat kii he
 The comments sarbajit ke parivaar ne maang kii he ki sarbajit ko bharat sarkaar shahid kaa darja de
 His daughter says Sarabjit was not a terrorist and should get his honor back
 is bich, punjab ke mukhyamantri prakaash singh badal ne is mudde par pradhanmantri se aaj subah baat kii or maang kii sarkaar ye koshish kare ki sarbajit kii hatya kii jaanch kisi antarrashtriya agency se ho
 The Punjab government has announced that the state government will provide government jobs to Sarabjit's daughters and they will be cremated with full state honors
 isse pehle air india ke vishesh vimaan se sarbajit ke shav ko amritsar ke hawaii adde par laayaa gaya

 amritsar hawaii adde par do kendriya mantri manish tiwari or paranit cor ke saath rajya sarkaar ke bhi kuch mantri va adhikari maujuud hai
 The Punjab government has announced a three-day state mourning
 punjab sarkaar ne ek karod rupee kii madad ke saath sarbajit kii donon betiyon ko sarkari naukari dene kii baat kahi he
 Apart from this, the Punjab government has also given martyr status to Sarabjit
 centre sarkaar kii ore se bhi 25 lakh rupee kii aarthik madad die jane kaa elaan kiya gaya he
 At the same time, there was news from Pakistan on Thursday evening that the Customs Department had stopped Sarabjit's body at the airport due to lack of some documents
 unka kahana tha ki videsh mantralay se abhi tak enosi nahin diya gaya he
 Later, after the completion of the paperwork, the aircraft flew with Sarabjit's body and about 7 at Amritsar airport
 30 baje pahunch gaya
 Sarabjit's last rites will be performed at around 2 pm with state honors on Friday
 saath hi kaha ja rahaa he ki antim sanskaar main pradhanmantri manmohan singh ke bhi aane kii sambhaavna he
 Apart from these, Congress Party Vice President Rahul Gandhi will also attend Sarabjit's funeral
 ullekhneey he ki kareeb ek saptaah tak jindagi or maut ke bich sangharsh karte hue sarbajit ne buudhvaar der raat 12:45 baje antim saans lee
 Sarabjit died of a heart attack at Jinnah Hospital in Lahore
 unki maut kadi suraksha vaali jail main kaidiyon dwaara barbar hamalaa kiye jane ke baad pichley chah dinon tak gahare coma main rahane ke baad hui
 The Pakistan government had constituted a panel of doctors for Sarabjit's postmortem
 pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne sarbajit singh kii maut par shok jataate hue kaha ki sarbajit par barbar or kaatilaanaa hamale ke jimmedaar aparaadhiyon ko nyaay ke kathghare main laayaa jaae
 The Ministry of External Affairs issued a press release saying that whatever happened to Sarabjit, the Indian government was deeply hurt
 bharat sarbajit par hamale ko ek bhartiya naagarik par hua kaatilaanaa hamalaa maanata he or chahta he ki paak sarkaar isaki nishpaksh jaanch karaae or doshiyon ke khilaaf sakht karrwai kare
 At the same time, the Ministry of External Affairs has also demanded to take steps from the government there to protect the security of Indian prisoners who are lodged in jails of Pakistan
 congress upaadhyaksh rahul gandhi ne sarbajit ke parivaar se mulaakaat kii
 Sources said that Gandhi spent around 40 minutes with Sarabjit's family and consoled him
 kendriya grahamantri susheel kumaar scindia ne bhi sarbajit ke parivaar se mulaakaat kii
 After meeting Sarabjit's sister Dalbir Kaur and other family members, Shinde told reporters that the funeral will be done according to the family's feelings after the body is found
 scindia ne kaha ki bharat 49-varshiya sarbajit ko behatar upachaar sunishchit karne ke liye aakhri samay tak pakistan se baat karata rahaa, lekin safalataa nahin mil saki
 He said that i have expressed my condolences to Sarabjit's sister from all over the country
 tippaniyan Sarabjit's family has demanded that the Government of India give Sarabjit martyr status
 unki beti kaa kahana he ki sarbajit aatankwaadi nahin the or unhen unka sammaan waapas milanaa chahie
 Meanwhile, Punjab Chief Minister Parkash Singh Badal spoke to the Prime Minister on the issue this morning and demanded that the government should try to investigate Sarabjit's murder from an international agency
